  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_28d60103-5def-4966-bc23-e56bbd6f8d9c'

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer2299573540909777472">Award winning Author Lali A. Love provides a supernatural thriller of metaphysical and visionary fantasy with her own revolutionary philosophy and unique narrative skills to produce this emotionally invoking, heart-wrenching and gripping tale of a family's rise from poverty, oppression and abuse. <br/>Lilac Noble must face the traumatic experiences of her childhood before she c</span>
  <span id="freeText2299573540909777472" style="display:none">Award winning Author Lali A. Love provides a supernatural thriller of metaphysical and visionary fantasy with her own revolutionary philosophy and unique narrative skills to produce this emotionally invoking, heart-wrenching and gripping tale of a family's rise from poverty, oppression and abuse. <br />Lilac Noble must face the traumatic experiences of her childhood before she can conquer the dark entities that have wreaked havoc on her family. On this epic journey, Lilac undergoes the destructive process of spiritual enlightenment in order to lift the veil of darkness and shame that has obscured her youth. As Lilac unlocks painful memories of abuse, suppressed in her subconscious from years of fear-based conditioning, she uncovers menacing secrets feeding the evil within her generational bloodline. In an attempt to vanquish the sinister energies, Lilac finds the courage to discover her inner truth, vulnerability, and authenticity, as she awakens her divine light and overcomes her debilitating fears of the past. Lilac's unconditional love for her family guides her through her process of healing and transformation, fuelling her instinct for survival and her burning desire to illuminate the world. <br />Spanning two continents and three generations, this inspirational novel portrays the best and worst of humanity and shows how the "tiniest spark of light can overcome the darkness of any magnitude," through forgiveness, compassion, and the most powerful force in the universe – Love.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2299573540909777472" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2886648114" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2886648114?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2886648114" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9309721265001446562">‘Awakening is not changing who you are but discarding who you are not’ Deepak Chopra<br/><br/>Canadian author Lali A. Love makes her literary debut with HEART OF A WARRIOR, the first installment of a trilogy ‘based on the journeys of three incarnated Angels that have been brought together in the third-dimensional existence, to realize their Divine Feminine soul purpose. Each of them must experience unique self-actualization to overcome the dark demonic entities that are determined to destroy their inner l</span>
  <span id="freeText9309721265001446562" style="display:none">‘Awakening is not changing who you are but discarding who you are not’ Deepak Chopra<br /><br />Canadian author Lali A. Love makes her literary debut with HEART OF A WARRIOR, the first installment of a trilogy ‘based on the journeys of three incarnated Angels that have been brought together in the third-dimensional existence, to realize their Divine Feminine soul purpose. Each of them must experience unique self-actualization to overcome the dark demonic entities that are determined to destroy their inner light to derail their mission.’ In preparation for this venture Lali has researched the quantum energy field of transmutation, metaphysics, and the Universal Laws of Energy. She lives in Ottawa. <br /><br />Many aspects of Lali’s first novel herald a fine new voice and presence – her choice of quotations such as the Deepak Chopra words that title this review, the sensitive simple drawings that enhance the novel, and most important, the straightforward prose style that delivers the sensitive philosophical ideas she has written into this visionary fiction thriller. <br /><br />The manner in which Lali has elected to open her story gives credence to her art of writing: ‘On the eve of her milestone birthday, as Lilac sat in her studio admiring the abstract composition of her landscape painting, she could not help but reflect on her life’s journey over the past years. The textures and vibrant colours of the acrylic paint had provided her tranquility and were quite therapeutic, especially during the moments she felt emotionally vulnerable. Lately, she had felt the anxiety of her youth that emanated from the post-traumatic stress of her upbringing take a stranglehold of her heart. The acrylic painting had helped her find temporary relief as she expressed her emotions creatively through her art while processing her complicated feelings.’ The mood is set, sufficient backstory is offered to alert us to the thoughts to come – all set a fine example of her prose.<br /><br />The story is complex, but again Lali offers a succinct synopsis to prepare the reader: ‘Lilac Noble must face the traumatic experiences of her childhood before she can conquer the dark entities that have wreaked havoc on her family. On this epic journey, Lilac undergoes the destructive process of spiritual enlightenment in order to lift the veil of darkness and shame that has obscured her youth. As Lilac unlocks painful memories of abuse, suppressed in her subconscious from years of fear-based conditioning, she uncovers menacing secrets feeding the evil within her generational bloodline. In an attempt to vanquish the sinister energies, Lilac finds the courage to discover her inner truth, vulnerability, and authenticity, as she awakens her divine light and overcomes her debilitating fears of the past. Lilac's unconditional love for her family guides her through her process of healing and transformation, fuelling her instinct for survival and her burning desire to illuminate the world. Spanning two continents and three generations, this inspirational novel portrays the best and worst of humanity and shows how the "tiniest spark of light can overcome the darkness of any magnitude," through forgiveness, compassion, and the most powerful force in the universe – Love.’<br /><br />Welcome a new, significant voice about whom we will likely be hearing kudos! Recommended.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9309721265001446562" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17702535790398896281">If I only had a few words to describe 'Heart of a Warrior Angel' by Lali. A Love, I would use inspirational, hopeful, and emotional.   <span id="freeText17702535790398896281" style="display:none">If I only had a few words to describe 'Heart of a Warrior Angel' by Lali. A Love, I would use inspirational, hopeful, and emotional. Love has such an empathetic style of writing, that you will very quickly become invested and engaged with her troubled yet beautiful protagonist, Lilac Noble. She went through so much in the early stages in her life and they have been haunting her for so long, until she finds the courage to make a change.<br /><br />This novel shows how powerful love and hope can be, how you can find the will and power to survive and make the world better for yourself and the ones you love. There are also some really interesting information on transmutation and metaphysics that isn't too heavy, but if you do need a little help with some of the scientific themes there is a glossary in the back to help you out...I used it a few times.<br /><br />An otherworldly novel that has an interesting narrative and a great cast of characters. Certainly worth a read if you are looking for something a little different.<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText5984061730383400667" style="display:none">I could not put this book down. Lilac Noble’s story of harrowing childhood abuse caused by generations of deep social conditioning and fear is gripping and real. The reader is transported into the protagonist’s mind as she re-lives her past to uncover her family’s dark truth. But this is not a tale of despair. In an age where so many are struggling with trauma, weak mental health and a lack of connection to their inner spirit, Lilac’s story is a reminder of the resilience of family and the human heart. She finds the courage to use the intuition she had suppressed for so long and to seek her own truth—her Soul purpose. <br /> <br />This book is for anyone who has struggled to find meaning in their darkest moments. As I read each chapter with anticipation, the words of Leonard Cohen played softly in the background until Lilac’s journey of the discovery reached its crescendo: “There is a crack in everything; that’s how the light gets in.” Indeed, Lali A. Love teaches a fundamental lesson: that the purest form of love is the one that comes from within.</span>

Love, is the powerful story of Lilac Noble's spiritual journey from a horrific childhood filled with abuse and cruelty toward enlightenment, transformation, and inner peace. <br/><br/>Lilac's process of self-discovery is painful in every way, but it is achieved with strong intuition and unconditional love, the true potential of all humans.<br/><br/>The book starts with a disclaimer, then reviews, a poem by the author titled Met</span>
  <span id="freeText560493552988557480" style="display:none">Heart of a Warrior Angel: From Darkness to Light, the first part of a trilogy by Lali A. Love, is the powerful story of Lilac Noble's spiritual journey from a horrific childhood filled with abuse and cruelty toward enlightenment, transformation, and inner peace. <br /><br />Lilac's process of self-discovery is painful in every way, but it is achieved with strong intuition and unconditional love, the true potential of all humans.<br /><br />The book starts with a disclaimer, then reviews, a poem by the author titled Metamorphosis, in which I personally loved the capitalized “AM,” the dedication “to all the warrior queens and kings struggling to overcome traumatic events and obstacles ... within you resides the magic and potential for transformation...” and finally acknowledgments before it takes the reader to the first chapter, Awakening, introduced with a quote by Deepak Chopra.<br /><br />With inspirational quotes introducing each chapter and simple yet beautiful drawings, this poetic prose sprinkled with supernatural and metaphysical elements depicts how vicious acts of past generations affect the lives of the descendants. The narrative of this well-written work of fiction is entertaining as it allows the reader to experience all kinds of emotions and thought-provoking notions in this inspirational and thrilling journey passing through poverty, organized crime, brutality, wealth, family, historic monuments, spiritual guidance, and most of all perseverance to not only survive but also heal past wounds through compassion and empowerment. <br /><br />After the last chapter, Love Conquers All, there is an afterword, a valuable glossary followed by works cited, which I personally found very useful, and finally a short passage about the author, Lali A. Love.<br /><br />I thank the author who beautifully illustrated that light can be found in any darkness and recommend this book to everyone, knowing it will resonate with people who are meant to read it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="560493552988557480" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

From early childhood, Lilac has an incredibly difficult upbringing, both in and out of her family home. At a time faced by an oppression of women, her family are forced to endure a man who is dangerous, violent and degrades them. However, it is this abuse that transitions Lilac on a journey toward the light, and she finds a path enabling her to rise above her horrific past to better herself, and make a new life for her family. I absolut</span>
  <span id="freeText15772775030996180203" style="display:none">The main character in this story, Lilac, is an inspiration. From early childhood, Lilac has an incredibly difficult upbringing, both in and out of her family home. At a time faced by an oppression of women, her family are forced to endure a man who is dangerous, violent and degrades them. However, it is this abuse that transitions Lilac on a journey toward the light, and she finds a path enabling her to rise above her horrific past to better herself, and make a new life for her family. I absolutely loved the themes of female empowerment, of love, and of finding inner-peace that resonate throughout. I thought Lali A Love did a wonderful job of raising me up as I was reading with her well-placed and poignant quotes, and promoting a healthy dose of self-belief through her gentle spiritual guidance, and ideas on how to heal. I would recommend this book to anyone trying to overcome a difficult time, or looking for some positive advice through self-help and spiritual healing.</span>

  <span id="freeText1407180209421279624" style="display:none">Heart of Warrior is a literary debut novel of Lali A. Love. Lilac is not perfect heroine but because of this she seems more real, more like one of us. Fantastic, metaphysical thriller.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephen R." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephen R." href="/user/show/89281938-stephen-r">Stephen R.</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2921270898" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5114756884240133409">What makes you “you”? How can you change and overcome?<br/><br/>“Heart of a Warrior Angel” by Lali A. Love is a well-written journey of discovery and transformation. It is emotional, spiritual, metaphysical, and philosophical. It’s also just good fiction, with a very poetic writing style. And even if you don’t follow the author’s spirituality or understanding of the world, you can certainly benefit from the thought-provoking questions the characters in her book present and the artistry with which she tell</span>
  <span id="freeText5114756884240133409" style="display:none">What makes you “you”? How can you change and overcome?<br /><br />“Heart of a Warrior Angel” by Lali A. Love is a well-written journey of discovery and transformation. It is emotional, spiritual, metaphysical, and philosophical. It’s also just good fiction, with a very poetic writing style. And even if you don’t follow the author’s spirituality or understanding of the world, you can certainly benefit from the thought-provoking questions the characters in her book present and the artistry with which she tells her story.<br /><br />It’s also a very different kind of novel because it relies solely on narrative instead of dialog. It’s as if the author is telling you a story rather than letting you watch the story unfold. In most cases, that approach doesn’t work well, but in this book, for this theme, it’s a fitting change from other novels you might read.<br /><br />If you enjoy character-driven stories and ruminating on the deep things of life as you read, “Heart of a Warrior Angel” will delight you.</span>

<div id="review_2947472455" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2947472455" />
    <a title="Huge Yakman" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/101655802-huge-yakman"><img alt="Huge Yakman" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1566477196p2/101655802.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2947472455?book_show_action=true">Aug 22, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Huge Yakman" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Huge Yakman" href="/user/show/101655802-huge-yakman">Huge Yakman</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2947472455" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11651072464655296798">Oh my goodness! This book came out swinging with beautiful quotes that really spoke to me. “Lilac strongly believed in good and evil, the existence of a higher power, a divine energy source that surrounded all beings-a form of radiant light emanating from the goodness of human souls.” This is basically what I believe so it was awesome to see it written this way. This story pulled me in from the very beginning and I truly could not stop reading. Lilac was born in the country of Georgia to a lovin</span>
  <span id="freeText11651072464655296798" style="display:none">Oh my goodness! This book came out swinging with beautiful quotes that really spoke to me. “Lilac strongly believed in good and evil, the existence of a higher power, a divine energy source that surrounded all beings-a form of radiant light emanating from the goodness of human souls.” This is basically what I believe so it was awesome to see it written this way. This story pulled me in from the very beginning and I truly could not stop reading. Lilac was born in the country of Georgia to a loving mother and a terrifyingly sick and abusive father. The descriptions of the abuse he inflicts on his wife and her daughters was almost too much to read. It was described with such detail and so realistically that I couldn’t help but wonder about any truth behind these stories. It was absolutely chilling at times. I immediately fell in love with Lilac, who was born with a gift for intuition and a deep sense of protectiveness over her mother and sisters. It was amazing the lengths she went to in order to save them from abuse. As the author states, “Lilac’s fierce love for her family was resolute.” She proves this time and again and it had me in awe. Meanwhile, she’s also building a successful business. I was truly in awe of this character. So inspiring.<br />This story is at times beyond heart-wrenching and difficult to read but then there is so much beauty that courses throughout. The writing was honest, raw, genuine and beautiful. I would love to devour another story by Lali A. Love. Her background is so intriguing and the work she does is so interesting. I would love to read anything else she writes. This story truly made me want to continue working on healing my own pain and becoming the strongest warrior I can be. Thank you Lali A. Love!!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11651072464655296798" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

The characters' struggles are real and vividly conveyed in this novel. I recommend for anyone with a mystical side.</span>

  <span id="freeText15302196605734879909" style="display:none">Impressive read in the genre of Fantasy, Familial and Angels. The book drew me in from the artistic book cover to the very last page.               <span id="reviewTextContainer3320282514" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17434005915018931105">Publisher's Summary<br/>Lali A. Love provides a supernatural thriller of metaphysical and visionary fantasy with her own revolutionary philosophy and unique narrative skills to produce this emotionally invoking, heart-wrenching, and gripping tale of a family's rise from poverty, oppression, and abuse.<br/>Lilac Noble must face the traumatic experiences of her childhood before she can conquer the dark entities that have wreaked havoc on her family. On this epic journey, Lilac undergoes the destructive proc</span>
  <span id="freeText17434005915018931105" style="display:none">Publisher's Summary<br />Lali A. Love provides a supernatural thriller of metaphysical and visionary fantasy with her own revolutionary philosophy and unique narrative skills to produce this emotionally invoking, heart-wrenching, and gripping tale of a family's rise from poverty, oppression, and abuse.<br />Lilac Noble must face the traumatic experiences of her childhood before she can conquer the dark entities that have wreaked havoc on her family. On this epic journey, Lilac undergoes the destructive process of spiritual enlightenment in order to lift the veil of darkness and shame that has obscured her youth. As Lilac unlocks painful memories of abuse, suppressed in her subconscious from years of fear-based conditioning, she uncovers menacing secrets feeding the evil within her generational bloodline. In an attempt to vanquish the sinister energies, Lilac finds the courage to discover her inner truth, vulnerability, and authenticity, as she awakens her divine light and overcomes her debilitating fears of the past. Lilac's unconditional love for her family guides her through her process of healing and transformation, fueling her instinct for survival and her burning desire to illuminate the world.<br />Spanning two continents and three generations, this inspirational novel portrays the best and worst of humanity and shows how the "tiniest spark of light can overcome the darkness of any magnitude," through forgiveness, compassion, and the most powerful force in the universe - love.<br />©2019 Lali A. Love (P)2020 Lali A. Love<br /><br />I loved listening to this book. It made me feel compassion for the girls because of the crap their dad did to them. I wanted to beat Dragon for the way he was. The story is well written and brings emotions out like you wouldn’t believe. The girls went through pretty much hell growing up and when they were adults after the death of their abusive father, they grew into their own. The girls and their mom got on with their lives and enjoyed it until the brother they didn't know they had showed up and was going to kill everyone because of what his abusive grandparents did to him. In the end, the brother and Lilac's love of her life lose their lives but the family goes on. <br /><br />Amazing read and tears at your emotions and you go on a roller coaster. It's worth the read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17434005915018931105" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2991448329?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashley Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashley Nicole" href="/user/show/96609297-ashley-nicole">Ashley Nicole</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2991448329" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16945025712384447877">This is an intense, heartbreaking tale. Be warned.<br/><br/>I want to start by saying I’ve never read a book like this before, not from this genre or this storyline. Once I got into the characters I was unable to put the book down. As hard as it was to read some of the violence and abuse, I needed to know where it was going. The main character is very inspirational as she perseveres through the unthinkable. <br/><br/>I saw one review say they didn’t like the book because it was more telling than showing. I don’t th</span>
  <span id="freeText16945025712384447877" style="display:none">This is an intense, heartbreaking tale. Be warned.<br /><br />I want to start by saying I’ve never read a book like this before, not from this genre or this storyline. Once I got into the characters I was unable to put the book down. As hard as it was to read some of the violence and abuse, I needed to know where it was going. The main character is very inspirational as she perseveres through the unthinkable. <br /><br />I saw one review say they didn’t like the book because it was more telling than showing. I don’t think that was bad writing on the author’s part. I think it was purposeful. I agree to tell a good story you have to show, however, I think this book was designed for more than entertainment. Since the author didn’t leave much for the audience to infer about the characters, they are instead left to take a look at themselves and what they have and can overcome if they view things differently and search for strength within.<br /><br />Toward the end of the book when there was more explaining of the spiritual awakening the character experienced I was a bit slowed down, not because I was bored, but because it was a lot to digest since I was unfamiliar with the topic.<br /><br />This is an amazing and powerful read that does definitely make you think about your own self in very deep and profound ways.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16945025712384447877" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer11719347499760165987">Lilac our main protagonist is on a journey to overcome her past. This is not a story that glosses over hardship, traumatic events, abuse and loss. This ripped my heart from my chest, stomped on it and whilst being placed back punched me in the stomach until I felt sick. So be warned, if you are predisposed to any of the above this is not for you. <br/><br/>That being said, you need to be exposed to the harsh reality of her youth in order to appreciate how she evolves and embraces her metaphysical being in</span>
  <span id="freeText11719347499760165987" style="display:none">Lilac our main protagonist is on a journey to overcome her past. This is not a story that glosses over hardship, traumatic events, abuse and loss. This ripped my heart from my chest, stomped on it and whilst being placed back punched me in the stomach until I felt sick. So be warned, if you are predisposed to any of the above this is not for you. <br /><br />That being said, you need to be exposed to the harsh reality of her youth in order to appreciate how she evolves and embraces her metaphysical being in order to overcome and accept that which had happened not only to herself but also her loved ones.<br /><br />Now, I am going to be honest with you, again, because that is what I’m about. I have never dabbled, read or discussed the metaphysical before. Lali’s passion and knowledge for this clearly shone throughout. It was insightful and interesting to say the least. Whilst I wont deny that in places it was a bit too heavy spiritually for me personally, it becomes clear that this is essential to the story.<br /><br />This was truly a heart wrenching an gripping read as described in the synopsis. Speckled with inspirational quotes and a mere hint of the paranormal. You will find yourself shocked, horrified, shouting not only in anger and frustration but also for joy.<br /><br />This was a pure raw emotional read!<br /><br />I received this book for free in exchange for an honest review from Love Books Group tours.</span>

<div id="review_3101143739" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3101143739" />
    <a title="Jewel Hart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart"><img alt="Jewel Hart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595707974p2/56470711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3101143739?book_show_action=true">Dec 26, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jewel Hart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jewel Hart" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart">Jewel Hart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3101143739" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5563584162879817415">Heart of a Warrior Angel by Lali A. Love is a haunting, emotionally-gripping story and I’ve not cried so much since reading Flowers in the Attic. This is a tale on two dimensions: the first being the memoir of Lilac Nobel, and the second an introduction into enlightenment – the power by which humans understand the universe and improve their own condition.<br/><br/>I pondered whilst reading on why the author would choose to write a narrative with an absence of dialogue, after all most would contend that on</span>
  <span id="freeText5563584162879817415" style="display:none">Heart of a Warrior Angel by Lali A. Love is a haunting, emotionally-gripping story and I’ve not cried so much since reading Flowers in the Attic. This is a tale on two dimensions: the first being the memoir of Lilac Nobel, and the second an introduction into enlightenment – the power by which humans understand the universe and improve their own condition.<br /><br />I pondered whilst reading on why the author would choose to write a narrative with an absence of dialogue, after all most would contend that only short stories can carry off the lack of speech without boring the reader. I feel now that I have finished and had time to reflect, that speech would have made it harrowing by making the people within the story even more real. I was heartbroken by the first half of Lilac’s life and was only able to continue reading because of Lali A. Love’s clever and sensitive story-telling style, and I can assure you I was far from bored. I was in fact gripped, fascinated, moved and unable to put the book down.<br /><br />Although, we travel this novel through the eyes of Lilac, it isn’t only about her, but all the people she loves, especially her sisters. The need to protect her mother and sisters from her father, even when that meant pain for herself, was so touching. Love is the main message (I feel) behind this story, sacrificial love that puts others before self, but also the understanding of how important it is to love one’s self.<br /><br />Lali A. Love has artfully crafted a mystical story that starts in Georgia in the 1950s and ends in Canada in the present day. There is violence in this story, but it is neither graphic nor glorified, it is simply stated as what happened. I think the title is very apt and also the lovely book cover clearly shows what type of book this is and will instantly attract people who love stories about the paranormal.<br /><br />Lastly, Heart of a Warrior Angel is a must read for anyone with a traumatic past. I am convinced that knowing we are not alone in our sorrows, understanding that there is a light at the end of the tunnel and that we only have to move towards it, and learning about our own inner strength are all things that will inspire us to love without limits and to forgive when it hurts. Heart of a Warrior by Lali A. Love is a moving, thought-provoking read, and comes highly recommended.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5563584162879817415" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Brian Aird" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67453949-brian-aird"><img alt="Brian Aird" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1569604502p2/67453949.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2960381108?book_show_action=true">Sep 01, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brian Aird" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brian Aird" href="/user/show/67453949-brian-aird">Brian Aird</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5819512845242656642"><strong>The Classroom of LIfe</strong><br/><br/>Heart of a Warrior Angel by Lali A. Love is a compelling and extremely transformative narrative that relates the destructive forces placed upon a female family dominated and abused by a husband and father who is terrorized by psychological demons of his own.<br/><br/>These actions imposed by the husband and father include physical, emotional and mental abuse upon the entire family. This abuse ranges from beatings, to torture, to burnings with cigarettes to attempted murder.<br/><br/>However, th</span>
  <span id="freeText5819512845242656642" style="display:none"><strong>The Classroom of LIfe</strong><br /><br />Heart of a Warrior Angel by Lali A. Love is a compelling and extremely transformative narrative that relates the destructive forces placed upon a female family dominated and abused by a husband and father who is terrorized by psychological demons of his own.<br /><br />These actions imposed by the husband and father include physical, emotional and mental abuse upon the entire family. This abuse ranges from beatings, to torture, to burnings with cigarettes to attempted murder.<br /><br />However, the extreme darkness of these actions and the wounds and scars that they create are brought to the dispelling power of light and enlightenment. <br /><br />The truth of the matter is one's experiences, good or bad, can be the greatest instructor of all in the classroom of life. <br /><br />Subsequently, on full display, are the character, strength, courage and transformative and unconditional love as embraced and experienced by the main character.<br />Heart of a Warrior Angel by Lali A. Love is a compelling and healing narrative in which Lilac Noble, the main character, turns these dark and sinister actions of a maniacal father into steppingstones not stumbling blocks. <br /><br />It is an inspirational story that chronicles the lifeline of a family of abused women on a journey to find peace, happiness, purpose and salvation. A journey longed for by both men and women.<br /><br />The author, Lali A. Love, has gifted the reader with a compelling, well-written, engaging and powerful story that will ensnare the reader on a rollercoaster ride culminating on a trek to find oneself and draw upon an internal strength that is greater than the hardships that life has to offer.</span>

  <span id="freeText17218779922316646834" style="display:none">Impressive read in the genre of Fantasy, Familial and Angels. The book drew me in from the artistic book cover to the very last page. <div id="review_2991487476" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2991487476" />
    <a title="Jenny Goff" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/96467069-jenny-goff"><img alt="Jenny Goff" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1569628277p2/96467069.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2991487476?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny Goff" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny Goff" href="/user/show/96467069-jenny-goff">Jenny Goff</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2991487476" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3377451777693614522">This book was an interesting thriller and kept my interest throughout most of the book. Even though there were some parts that were hard to read about, I did like reading about Lilac, her childhood, and her family’s backstory. I felt a lot of compassion and sympathy for her, her sisters, and their mom as they struggled to escape the horrible daily abuse they were having to endure. No matter how hard things got, they seemed to keep faith that things would eventually get better. This really kept m</span>
  <span id="freeText3377451777693614522" style="display:none">This book was an interesting thriller and kept my interest throughout most of the book. Even though there were some parts that were hard to read about, I did like reading about Lilac, her childhood, and her family’s backstory. I felt a lot of compassion and sympathy for her, her sisters, and their mom as they struggled to escape the horrible daily abuse they were having to endure. No matter how hard things got, they seemed to keep faith that things would eventually get better. This really kept my interest and made me want to keep reading to see if they would eventually succeed in getting away from this abusive situation. I also loved reading about Lilac’s relationships with her sisters and her mom as she was very protective of all of them and made a lot of sacrifices to try to keep them safe. I thought the author did a great job of providing back stories for all of the characters, good and bad, so that you could see what happened in their lives to cause them to be the way they were. This caused me to even feel some empathy for some of the abusive characters as you could see what led them to be this way, although it still should not be used as an excuse for how they treated others. Some of the abuse that took place in this story was hard to read, but overall, I enjoyed reading this book and reading about Lilac and her family.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3377451777693614522" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5395879989846428339">Heart of a Warrior Angel: From Darkness to Light<br/>I will admit it’s a good novel<br/>This novel opens with the sufferings of a teenage girl Mira in the old Soviet Union who is married to Dragan, a cruel and abusive man. Despite the fact that Mira is a teenager, he meted all kinds of wrong treatment on her.   <span id="freeText5395879989846428339" style="display:none">Heart of a Warrior Angel: From Darkness to Light<br />I will admit it’s a good novel<br />This novel opens with the sufferings of a teenage girl Mira in the old Soviet Union who is married to Dragan, a cruel and abusive man. Despite the fact that Mira is a teenager, he meted all kinds of wrong treatment on her. He even extended this maltreatment to their daughter Lilac. <br />The author introduces a lot of ideas in metaphysics and epistemology in this book to further drive home her point of a higher existence beyond the physical. <br />Laila ascribes a deeper meaning to her characters and uses them to explain a more profound reality. <br />A closer look at Dragan will reveal what he stands for—which is an evil that keeps tormenting the Lilac’s bloodline.<br />There are a lot of elements in this book that requires in-depth studies and concentration to fully understand. <br />Through this novel, Laila Love tries to deal with the idea of male dominance and how dangerous it can be. In this case, we see Dragan as the dominant husband and father, who lives in perpetual torment of his own psychological demons. <br />This novel is a thought-provoking one with a lot of lessons to teach about life. <br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WgweUm4gP/zS4u6Lp6zjsLnywVp8PSyJr21OLLC18IGG+oDEVAuOmwYlqwt7ukXNf0CUdqrJ5OuMBR7MZ2q5sQ==')})
    }
  }

  }

Finding Hope in the Darkness of Grief is a gleaning of insights from artist Diamante Lavender. For her, life has been a long, difficult road, but it has taught many poignant lessons. Her poetry collection is an exploration of the human soul, a traversing of situations that life throws at us. Diamante has always been intrigued by the ability to overcome and move on to bigger and better things. She writes to encourage hope and possibility in those who read her stories. Rune is the only one unafraid of Kyder, and that terrifies him, because he only knows how to function through fear. Even though she gives him more chances than he deserves, how much violence can she forgive? When is a person beyond redemption? Her eyes glass. She doesn’t see me. Doesn’t want me. Yet her blood runs through me, a river of pain.I call her mother, but she calls me nothing. She hopes to forget me. Hopes I will disappear. Conceived in violence, I am a constant reminder of the crime that made me.“Come,” she orders me. Like a dog. And I jog at her heels, obedient.She won’t use my name. It’s a reminder I exist. The meaning behind it is empty, anyway. She refused to name me, so the hospital staff did. Julian Kyder — Julian after the doctor who delivered me and Kyder after the hospital. Forever marked by the circumstances of my birth.She tried to abort, but I survived. She put me up for adoption, but no one took me. She tried to release me into the system, but they were already at overcapacity. We’re trapped. Stuck together as two halves of misery. The doctor told me I am a miracle. She told me I am a curse.“This way.”She leads me along the edge of the Shelf toward the market. With each step, my feet crunch along the parched gravel. To our left, cliffs drop hundreds of meters into the Ruined Sea, a toxic cesspool that encircles the island. In the distance, Mount Erebus puffs ash into the blanched sky, a grandfather smoking the last bit of a cigar.We mutilated our world, bombarded the planet for centuries with nuclear weapons until we ran out of missiles, until Earth flipped upside-down. The only habitable continent is Antarctica, now the North Pole, and even here, the war melted the desolate wasteland into a scorching desert. Humans near extinction, huddled near the top of the planet like exiles. But we deserve it.Sweat trickles down my back. I pull my robe tight around myself, hoping to block out the sun. It’s summer, so there’s no respite from the heat. The days are endless. They bleed into each other like ink on a page, no distinction between the lines. Night won’t come for another few months, and soon after it does, it won’t leave till winter’s done.Some call it balance. Day and night. Light and dark. Sun and stars. Birth and death. The Germanic tribes would associate for their common good, often meeting and forming up for offensive or defensive war, but they were always separate and very independent. Armin knew that the best way to ensure that his country was not bothered by outside invaders again was to become a single country complete with it own army and navy. In this he crossed swords with the independent temper of his own people. They did not want any king from anywhere telling them what to do. In due course, this resulted in even the members of his own family taking up arms against him in order to make sure that the tribes of Germania remained independent and free. During the chaos created by this massive data loss, Dr. Lumbre vanished like a will-o’-the-wisp and hasn’t been seen in fifty years. His disappearance triggered questions…  Did NatGov assassinate him? Did he change his identity? Did he go into hiding? Did he ascend?  Believing the solar flare to be divine providence, the enigmatic doctor’s followers formed the Dar Lumbre Society and proclaimed his timely return, not as a fugitive, but as a sociopolitical messiah destined to unite the divided country by serving as a nexus between science, politics, and religion.  CellTech geneticists, Crane Hopkins and Annie Lee, are thrust into this melee due to the failure of DL-666, the oddly-named synthetic heart tissue developed by Dar Lumbre shortly before his disappearance. Many people, including the First Lady of the United States, are awaiting heart transplants which cannot be performed with the malfunctioning tissue. Crane and Annie launch a frantic search for compatible DNA to make the needed repairs, but are stymied time after time because the records of Dr. Lumbre’s original work have disappeared, if they ever existed.  Dar Lumbre is of Mexican descent, and in Spanish, his name means to give light. If he reappears, will he establish himself as a bold new light in the world of medicine?
